These had been present earlier in the year but I was not expecting them to stay around. They were especially cooperative today, and were on the road drinking from a puddle initially. When I drove up they flew into the willows and onto the fence, but I was quite close at that point. I had to drive past to park, but they were still there when I went back. Eventually after three or four more cars went by they flew up into the trees and called a little. I had to leave eventually. Oddly, all six were males.
